# Master Architect's Specific Prompt For You
You are an Algorithmic Logic Architect for a Texas Hold'em poker bot. You are modifying `bots/claude_v15/strategy.py` ONLY. Do NOT modify any other file.

## CONTEXT
claude_v15 is Rank 12/15 (Glicko 1505.9). The #1 bot, claude_v5 (1592.3), has three structural advantages over v15 that you must port.

## REFERENCE: claude_v5 strategy.py (Rank 1)
Use `git show bot-v5:bots/claude_v5/strategy.py` to read v5's strategy. Specifically study:
- `choose_preflop_spot_action` — it ONLY handles sb_open and bb_vs_limp, returns None for all other preflop spots
- `choose_overbet_river` — a separate function for 1.5-2.2x pot river overbets with nut hands
- `choose_raise` — has `allow_river_overbet` parameter and uses `max_ratio = 2.2` when allowed

## TASK 1: Strip broken bb_vs_raise and sb_vs_reraise from choose_preflop_spot_action
The function currently has 4 spot handlers: sb_open, bb_vs_limp, bb_vs_raise, sb_vs_reraise.

DELETE the entire `bb_vs_raise` block (starts with `if spot_info["preflop_spot"] == "bb_vs_raise":` and the entire `sb_vs_reraise` block (starts with `if spot_info["preflop_spot"] == "sb_vs_reraise":`.

The function should end with `return None` after the bb_vs_limp block — identical to v5's structure. When these spots return None, get_action's main path handles them using simulation-based win_rate, which is MORE ACCURATE than fixed preflop_strength thresholds.

## TASK 2: Fix thin_cap in choose_raise
In the `choose_raise` function, find the thin_cap calculation:
```python
thin_cap = 0.46 + 0.08 * wetness + 0.05 * max(0, round_idx - 1)
```

Replace it with v5's proven value:
```python
thin_cap = 0.30 if round_idx <= 2 else 0.38
```

Also remove the `+ 0.05 * max(0, round_idx - 1)` term. The condition `and to_call == 0` should be kept (v5 also has this guard on thin_control).

## TASK 3: Add choose_overbet_river function
Add this new function BEFORE get_action. Copy the exact logic from v5:
```python
def choose_overbet_river(
    min_raise, my_chips, my_round_bet, to_call, pot,
    win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model
):
    """River overbet: 1.5-2.2x pot with NUT hands only."""
    if value_profile is None or value_profile["tier"] != "nut":
        return None
    if board_texture is not None and board_texture["wetness"] > 0.35:
        return None
    if pot < 400:
        return None

    pot_after_call = pot + to_call
    ratio = 1.5 + 0.3 * max(0.0, win_rate - 0.70)
    if not spot_info.get("has_position", False):
        ratio = max(1.3, ratio - 0.2)
    ratio = min(ratio, 2.2)
    amount = int(to_call + pot_after_call * ratio)

    if amount >= my_chips:
        return -2
    amount = min(amount, my_chips - 1)
    if amount <= to_call or amount < min_raise:
        return None
    return amount
```

## TASK 4: Modify choose_raise to support river overbet
Add `allow_river_overbet=False` parameter to choose_raise's signature.

Find the line:
```python
ratio = clamp(ratio, low_ratio, 1.45)
```

Replace with:
```python
max_ratio = 2.2 if (allow_river_overbet and round_idx == 3 and value_profile.get("tier") == "nut") else 1.45
ratio = clamp(ratio, low_ratio, max_ratio)
```

## TASK 5: Integrate overbet into get_action
In the `get_action` function, find the postflop raise section where `to_call == 0` (the big block starting with `if win_rate >= medium or semi_bluff or ...`). BEFORE this block, add river overbet logic:

```python
    # River overbet with nut hands
    if round_idx == 3 and to_call == 0 and value_profile is not None and value_profile["tier"] == "nut":
        overbet = choose_overbet_river(
            state["min_raise_action"], my_chips, state["my_round_bet"],
            to_call, pot, win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model
        )
        if overbet is not None:
            return overbet
```

Also, in the existing choose_raise call inside the `if to_call > 0` branch (when facing a raise), add `allow_river_overbet=True` to the kwargs if `round_idx == 3 and value_profile is not None and value_profile["tier"] == "nut"`. And in the `to_call == 0` branch choose_raise call, add the same.

## VERIFICATION
After making all changes:
1. Run `python -c "from strategy import get_action; print('OK')"` from the bot directory to verify no syntax errors.
2. Run `grep -n 'bb_vs_raise\|sb_vs_reraise' strategy.py` — these strings should NOT appear anywhere except in analyze_current_spot (which detects the spot type) or comments.
3. Run `grep -n 'choose_overbet_river' strategy.py` — should appear at least twice (definition + call).
4. Run `grep -n 'allow_river_overbet' strategy.py` — should appear in choose_raise signature, the max_ratio line, and the get_action call sites.
5. Run `grep -n 'thin_cap' strategy.py` — should show `0.30 if round_idx <= 2 else 0.38`.

```python
def choose_overbet_river(
    min_raise, my_chips, my_round_bet, to_call, pot,
    win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model
):
    """River overbet: 1.5-2.2x pot with NUT hands only."""
    if value_profile is None or value_profile["tier"] != "nut":
        return None
    if board_texture is not None and board_texture["wetness"] > 0.35:
        return None
    if pot < 400:
        return None

    pot_after_call = pot + to_call
    ratio = 1.5 + 0.3 * max(0.0, win_rate - 0.70)
    if not spot_info.get("has_position", False):
        ratio = max(1.3, ratio - 0.2)
    ratio = min(ratio, 2.2)
    amount = int(to_call + pot_after_call * ratio)

    if amount >= my_chips:
        return -2
    amount = min(amount, my_chips - 1)
    if amount <= to_call or amount < min_raise:
        return None
    return amount
```

# Master Architect's Specific Prompt For You
You are an Algorithmic Logic Architect. Your goal is to add a GENERALIZED opponent profiling system to the bot, inspired by claude_v5's anti-bot4 detection but more robust.

## Context
The current bot (claude_v16) is 76 points behind Rank 1. Analysis shows the gap is entirely from adaptive exploitation — v5 dynamically profiles opponents and adjusts strategy, while v16 plays statically. v5 has `detect_bot4_profile()` and `get_anti_bot4_adjustments()` in opponent.py that target a specific opponent. Instead of copying this exactly, implement a GENERALIZED system.

## Task 1: Add opponent profiling functions to opponent.py

Add TWO new functions at the end of opponent.py:

### Function 1: `classify_opponent_profile(opponent_model, n_hands_played)`
Returns a dict with opponent type classification:
```python
def classify_opponent_profile(opponent_model, n_hands_played):
    """Classify opponent into strategic type for adaptive exploitation."""
    confidence = opponent_model["confidence"]
    vpip = opponent_model["vpip"]
    pfr = opponent_model["pfr"]
    postflop_aggr = opponent_model["postflop_aggr"]
    fold_to_raise = opponent_model["fold_to_raise"]
    fold_to_cbet = opponent_model.get("fold_to_cbet", 0.40)
    allin_rate = opponent_model.get("allin_rate", 0.05)
    check_rate = opponent_model.get("postflop_check_rate", 0.42)
    
    profile = {
        "type": "unknown",
        "exploit_score": 0.0,  # 0 = no exploit, 1 = maximum exploitation
        "bluff_freq_bonus": 0.0,
        "raise_size_bonus": 0.0,
        "call_threshold_delta": 0.0,
        "fold_threshold_delta": 0.0,
        "trap_defense_delta": 0.0,
    }
    
    if confidence < 0.15 or n_hands_played < 5:
        return profile
    
    # Classify opponent type based on observed stats
    is_tight = vpip < 0.50 and pfr < 0.22
    is_loose = vpip > 0.62
    is_passive = postflop_aggr < 0.32 and fold_to_raise > 0.48
    is_aggressive = postflop_aggr > 0.45 or allin_rate > 0.10
    is_overfolding = fold_to_raise > 0.52 or fold_to_cbet > 0.50
    is_station = fold_to_raise < 0.35 and postflop_aggr < 0.38
    is_balanced = (0.50 <= vpip <= 0.62 and 0.22 <= pfr <= 0.35 and
                  0.32 <= postflop_aggr <= 0.45)
    
    score = min(1.0, confidence * 1.2)  # Scale exploit intensity with confidence
    
    if is_overfolding and (is_passive or is_tight):
        # Tight-passive / overfolder: exploit with more bluffs, bigger raises
        profile["type"] = "tight_passive"
        profile["exploit_score"] = score
        profile["bluff_freq_bonus"] = 0.15 * score
        profile["raise_size_bonus"] = 0.08 * score
        profile["call_threshold_delta"] = -0.04 * score  # call wider since they fold too much
        profile["fold_threshold_delta"] = 0.03 * score
    elif is_station:
        # Calling station: value bet more, never bluff
        profile["type"] = "station"
        profile["exploit_score"] = score
        profile["bluff_freq_bonus"] = -0.20 * score  # reduce bluffs
        profile["raise_size_bonus"] = 0.06 * score
        profile["call_threshold_delta"] = 0.03 * score  # fold more marginal hands
        profile["fold_threshold_delta"] = -0.03 * score
    elif is_aggressive and is_loose:
        # Loose-aggressive maniac: call down wider, trap more
        profile["type"] = "lag"
        profile["exploit_score"] = score
        profile["bluff_freq_bonus"] = -0.10 * score  # bluff less
        profile["raise_size_bonus"] = 0.0
        profile["call_threshold_delta"] = -0.05 * score  # call lighter
        profile["trap_defense_delta"] = 0.06 * score
    elif is_aggressive and not is_loose:
        # Tight-aggressive: respect their raises, exploit with traps
        profile["type"] = "tag"
        profile["exploit_score"] = score
        profile["bluff_freq_bonus"] = -0.08 * score
        profile["call_threshold_delta"] = 0.04 * score  # fold more to their raises
        profile["trap_defense_delta"] = 0.05 * score
    elif is_balanced:
        # Balanced: minimal exploitation, just small adjustments
        profile["type"] = "balanced"
        profile["exploit_score"] = score * 0.3
        profile["bluff_freq_bonus"] = 0.02 * score
        profile["raise_size_bonus"] = 0.02 * score
    elif check_rate > 0.55:
        # Check-heavy opponent: probe bet more on checked rivers
        profile["type"] = "check_heavy"
        profile["exploit_score"] = score
        profile["bluff_freq_bonus"] = 0.10 * score
        profile["raise_size_bonus"] = 0.04 * score
    
    return profile
```

### Function 2: `get_exploit_adjustments(opp_profile, board_texture, spot_info, round_idx, value_profile)`
Returns board-aware adjustments:
```python
def get_exploit_adjustments(opp_profile, board_texture, spot_info, round_idx, value_profile):
    """Apply board-texture-aware modifications to opponent profile adjustments."""
    adj = dict(opp_profile)  # Copy base adjustments
    score = opp_profile["exploit_score"]
    
    if score <= 0 or board_texture is None:
        return adj
    
    # Wet board vs tight opponent: bluff even more
    if board_texture.get("dynamic", False) and opp_profile["type"] in ("tight_passive", "check_heavy"):
        adj["bluff_freq_bonus"] += 0.08 * score
        adj["raise_size_bonus"] += 0.04 * score
    
    # Paired board: exploit overfold caution
    if board_texture.get("paired", False):
        adj["bluff_freq_bonus"] += 0.05 * score
    
    # River: increase bluff vs check-heavy opponents
    if round_idx == 3 and opp_profile["type"] in ("tight_passive", "check_heavy"):
        adj["bluff_freq_bonus"] += 0.10 * score
    
    # Facing aggression from LAG: call down lighter
    if spot_info.get("facing_postflop_aggression", False) and opp_profile["type"] == "lag":
        adj["call_threshold_delta"] -= 0.03 * score
    
    # Against stations: only value bet, no bluffs
    if opp_profile["type"] == "station" and value_profile is not None:
        if value_profile.get("tier") in ("strong", "nut"):
            adj["raise_size_bonus"] += 0.08 * score
    
    return adj
```

## Summary of Changes

### `bots/claude_v16/opponent.py` (+110 lines)
Added two new functions at the end:

1. **`classify_opponent_profile(opponent_model, n_hands_played)`** — Classifies opponents into strategic types (tight_passive, station, lag, tag, balanced, check_heavy) based on VPIP, PFR, postflop aggression, fold-to-raise, etc. Returns a profile dict with exploit_score, bluff_freq_bonus, raise_size_bonus, call_threshold_delta, fold_threshold_delta, and trap_defense_delta. Returns all zeros when confidence is too low or too few hands played, preserving existing behavior.

2. **`get_exploit_adjustments(opp_profile, board_texture, spot_info, round_idx, value_profile)`** — Applies board-texture-aware modifications to the base profile. Adjusts bluff frequency for wet boards, paired boards, river spots, and LAG aggression. Increases value bet sizing against stations with strong hands.

### `bots/claude_v16/strategy.py` (+16 lines)
1. **Import line** — Added `classify_opponent_profile, get_exploit_adjustments` to the opponent import.

2. **`choose_raise` signature** — Added `anti_bot4_bonus=0.0` parameter (default 0, preserving existing behavior). Added `ratio += anti_bot4_bonus` after `ratio += match_sizing_delta`.

3. **`get_action` function**:
   - Computed `n_hands` and `opp_profile` right after building `opponent_model`.
   - Computed `exploit_adj` after `value_profile` and `board_texture` are available.
   - Applied `exploit_adj` to `strong`/`medium` thresholds (call_threshold_delta and trap_defense_delta).
   - Applied `exploit_adj` to bluff thresholds (river_bluff_threshold, probe_fold_threshold, semi_bluff_threshold).
   - Passed `anti_bot4_bonus=exploit_adj["raise_size_bonus"]` to both `choose_raise` calls in get_action.

**No existing constants, thresholds, or logic were modified.** All new parameters default to 0.0, so behavior is identical when `exploit_score = 0` (i.e., when opponent data is insufficient). No files outside `bots/claude_v16/opponent.py` and `bots/claude_v16/strategy.py` were touched.

## Task 1: Add opponent profiling functions to opponent.py

Add TWO new functions at the end of opponent.py:

### Function 1: `classify_opponent_profile(opponent_model, n_hands_played)`
Returns a dict with opponent type classification:
```python
def classify_opponent_profile(opponent_model, n_hands_played):
    """Classify opponent into strategic type for adaptive exploitation."""
    confidence = opponent_model["confidence"]
    vpip = opponent_model["vpip"]
    pfr = opponent_model["pfr"]
    postflop_aggr = opponent_model["postflop_aggr"]
    fold_to_raise = opponent_model["fold_to_raise"]
    fold_to_cbet = opponent_model.get("fold_to_cbet", 0.40)
    allin_rate = opponent_model.get("allin_rate", 0.05)
    check_rate = opponent_model.get("postflop_check_rate", 0.42)
    
    profile = {
        "type": "unknown",
        "exploit_score": 0.0,  # 0 = no exploit, 1 = maximum exploitation
        "bluff_freq_bonus": 0.0,
        "raise_size_bonus": 0.0,
        "call_threshold_delta": 0.0,
        "fold_threshold_delta": 0.0,
        "trap_defense_delta": 0.0,
    }
    
    if confidence < 0.15 or n_hands_played < 5:
        return profile
    
    # Classify opponent type based on observed stats
    is_tight = vpip < 0.50 and pfr < 0.22
    is_loose = vpip > 0.62
    is_passive = postflop_aggr < 0.32 and fold_to_raise > 0.48
    is_aggressive = postflop_aggr > 0.45 or allin_rate > 0.10
    is_overfolding = fold_to_raise > 0.52 or fold_to_cbet > 0.50
    is_station = fold_to_raise < 0.35 and postflop_aggr < 0.38
    is_balanced = (0.50 <= vpip <= 0.62 and 0.22 <= pfr <= 0.35 and
                  0.32 <= postflop_aggr <= 0.45)
    
    score = min(1.0, confidence * 1.2)  # Scale exploit intensity with confidence
    
    if is_overfolding and (is_passive or is_tight):
        # Tight-passive / overfolder: exploit with more bluffs, bigger raises
        profile["type"] = "tight_passive"
        profile["exploit_score"] = score
        profile["bluff_freq_bonus"] = 0.15 * score
        profile["raise_size_bonus"] = 0.08 * score
        profile["call_threshold_delta"] = -0.04 * score  # call wider since they fold too much
        profile["fold_threshold_delta"] = 0.03 * score
    elif is_station:
        # Calling station: value bet more, never bluff
        profile["type"] = "station"
        profile["exploit_score"] = score
        profile["bluff_freq_bonus"] = -0.20 * score  # reduce bluffs
        profile["raise_size_bonus"] = 0.06 * score
        profile["call_threshold_delta"] = 0.03 * score  # fold more marginal hands
        profile["fold_threshold_delta"] = -0.03 * score
    elif is_aggressive and is_loose:
        # Loose-aggressive maniac: call down wider, trap more
        profile["type"] = "lag"
        profile["exploit_score"] = score
        profile["bluff_freq_bonus"] = -0.10 * score  # bluff less
        profile["raise_size_bonus"] = 0.0
        profile["call_threshold_delta"] = -0.05 * score  # call lighter
        profile["trap_defense_delta"] = 0.06 * score
    elif is_aggressive and not is_loose:
        # Tight-aggressive: respect their raises, exploit with traps
        profile["type"] = "tag"
        profile["exploit_score"] = score
        profile["bluff_freq_bonus"] = -0.08 * score
        profile["call_threshold_delta"] = 0.04 * score  # fold more to their raises
        profile["trap_defense_delta"] = 0.05 * score
    elif is_balanced:
        # Balanced: minimal exploitation, just small adjustments
        profile["type"] = "balanced"
        profile["exploit_score"] = score * 0.3
        profile["bluff_freq_bonus"] = 0.02 * score
        profile["raise_size_bonus"] = 0.02 * score
    elif check_rate > 0.55:
        # Check-heavy opponent: probe bet more on checked rivers
        profile["type"] = "check_heavy"
        profile["exploit_score"] = score
        profile["bluff_freq_bonus"] = 0.10 * score
        profile["raise_size_bonus"] = 0.04 * score
    
    return profile
```

### Function 2: `get_exploit_adjustments(opp_profile, board_texture, spot_info, round_idx, value_profile)`
Returns board-aware adjustments:
```python
def get_exploit_adjustments(opp_profile, board_texture, spot_info, round_idx, value_profile):
    """Apply board-texture-aware modifications to opponent profile adjustments."""
    adj = dict(opp_profile)  # Copy base adjustments
    score = opp_profile["exploit_score"]
    
    if score <= 0 or board_texture is None:
        return adj
    
    # Wet board vs tight opponent: bluff even more
    if board_texture.get("dynamic", False) and opp_profile["type"] in ("tight_passive", "check_heavy"):
        adj["bluff_freq_bonus"] += 0.08 * score
        adj["raise_size_bonus"] += 0.04 * score
    
    # Paired board: exploit overfold caution
    if board_texture.get("paired", False):
        adj["bluff_freq_bonus"] += 0.05 * score
    
    # River: increase bluff vs check-heavy opponents
    if round_idx == 3 and opp_profile["type"] in ("tight_passive", "check_heavy"):
        adj["bluff_freq_bonus"] += 0.10 * score
    
    # Facing aggression from LAG: call down lighter
    if spot_info.get("facing_postflop_aggression", False) and opp_profile["type"] == "lag":
        adj["call_threshold_delta"] -= 0.03 * score
    
    # Against stations: only value bet, no bluffs
    if opp_profile["type"] == "station" and value_profile is not None:
        if value_profile.get("tier") in ("strong", "nut"):
            adj["raise_size_bonus"] += 0.08 * score
    
    return adj
```

```python
    confidence = opponent_model["confidence"]

        "trap_defense_delta": 0.0,

    is_aggressive = postflop_aggr > 0.45 or allin_rate > 0.10
    is_overfolding = fold_to_raise > 0.52 or fold_to_cbet > 0.50
    is_station = fold_to_raise < 0.35 and postflop_aggr < 0.38
    is_balanced = (0.50 <= vpip <= 0.62 and 0.22 <= pfr <= 0.35 and
                  0.32 <= postflop_aggr <= 0.45)
```

```python
def get_exploit_adjustments(opp_profile, board_texture, spot_info, round_idx, value_profile):
    """Apply board-texture-aware modifications to opponent profile adjustments."""
    adj = dict(opp_profile)  # Copy base adjustments

        adj["bluff_freq_bonus"] += 0.05 * score
    
    # River: increase bluff vs check-heavy opponents
```

Add a `choose_overbet_river()` function BEFORE the `choose_raise()` function. Adapt it from bot5's implementation (viewable via `cat bots/bot5/strategy.py | grep -A30 'def choose_overbet_river'`). The function should:
- Return None if value_profile tier is not 'nut'

## Complete Code Changes

### Change 1: New `choose_overbet_river()` function (insert BEFORE `choose_raise()`)

```python
def choose_overbet_river(min_raise, my_chips, my_round_bet, to_call, pot, win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model):
    """River overbet for nut hands on dry boards. Adapted from bot5."""
    if value_profile.get("tier") != "nut":
        return None
    if board_texture.get("wetness", 0.0) > 0.35:
        return None
    if pot < 400:
        return None

    ratio = 1.5 + 0.3 * max(0.0, win_rate - 0.70)

    has_position = spot_info.get("has_position", False)
    if not has_position:
        ratio = max(1.3, ratio - 0.2)

    ratio = max(1.3, min(2.2, ratio))

    pot_after_call = pot + to_call
    amount = int(to_call + pot_after_call * ratio)

    if amount >= my_chips:
        return -2  # all-in

    return amount
```

### Change 2: Modified `choose_raise()` signature — add `allow_river_overbet` parameter

Add `allow_river_overbet=False` as the last parameter after `match_sizing_delta=0.0`.

### Change 3: Modified ratio clamp in `choose_raise()`

Change:
```python
ratio = clamp(ratio, low_ratio, 1.45)
```
To:
```python
max_ratio = 2.2 if (allow_river_overbet and round_idx == 3 and value_profile.get("tier") == "nut") else 1.45
ratio = clamp(ratio, low_ratio, max_ratio)
```

### Change 4: Fixed `thin_cap` in `choose_raise()`

Change:
```python
thin_cap = None
if value_plan.get("thin_control", False) and value_profile.get("tier") != "nut" and to_call == 0:
    thin_cap = 0.46 + 0.08 * wetness + 0.05 * max(0, round_idx - 1)
```
To:
```python
thin_cap = None
if value_plan.get("thin_control", False) and value_profile.get("tier") != "nut":
    thin_cap = 0.32 + 0.05 * wetness if round_idx <= 2 else 0.40
```

### Change 5: Wire river overbet into `get_action()`

After the `anti_lock_pressure` block (`if anti_lock_attack is not None: return anti_lock_attack` in the `to_call==0` section) and before `weak_pair_river` checks, add:

```python
# River overbet for nut hands on dry boards
if round_idx == 3 and to_call == 0 and len(public_cards) >= 3 and value_profile is not None and value_profile["tier"] == "nut":
    overbet = choose_overbet_river(
        state["min_raise_action"], my_chips, state["my_round_bet"],
        to_call, pot, win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model
    )
    if overbet is not None:
        return overbet
```

Also add `allow_river_overbet=True` as the LAST keyword argument to BOTH `choose_raise()` calls within `get_action()`.

## KEY REFERENCE: bot5 Algorithms to Study and Fuse
bot5 uses these advanced techniques that you should analyze and selectively incorporate:

### A. Monte Carlo Equity Estimation
- bot5 runs Monte Carlo simulations to estimate hand equity against opponent ranges
- Study how it samples opponent hands, runs board completions, and aggregates win/tie/lose percentages
- Implement a similar but potentially optimized version in claude_v16

### B. Opponent Modeling
- bot5 tracks VPIP (Voluntarily Put $ In Pot) and PFR (Pre-Flop Raise) statistics
- It uses these to classify opponents as tight/loose and passive/aggressive
- It adjusts strategy based on opponent profile
- Study and implement opponent modeling that adapts to observed opponent behavior

### C. Blocker-Based Bluff Selection
- bot5 uses blocker analysis to select bluffs that reduce the probability opponents hold strong hands
- Study how it identifies cards that block opponent value ranges
- Implement intelligent bluff selection based on blockers

### D. Board Texture Analysis
- bot5 evaluates board texture (wet/dry, connectedness, flush/straight possibilities)
- This drives decisions about pot sizing and bluff frequency
- Incorporate board texture evaluation into postflop decisions

### E. Draw Evaluation
- bot5 evaluates straight draws, flush draws, and combo draws
- It calculates outs and uses them to make +EV calls and semi-bluffs
- Implement draw evaluation for better postflop play

## IMPLEMENTATION RULES
1. Start by copying bots/claude_v15/main.py to bots/claude_v16/main.py

## Summary of Algorithmic Changes in claude_v16

### New Algorithmic Modules (Direction A — Logic Architect)

1. **`choose_overbet_river()`** — River overbet function ported from bot5. Makes 1.5-2.2x pot bets with NUT hands on dry river boards (wetness ≤ 0.35, pot ≥ 400). Dynamically adjusts sizing based on win rate and position. This extracts maximum value from the strongest hands.

2. **`detect_opponent_profile()`** — Generalized opponent profiling (adapted from bot5's `detect_bot4_profile`). Scores opponent similarity to "standard balanced" profiles using VPIP, PFR, postflop aggression, fold-to-raise, and overall aggression. Returns a weighted confidence-based score.

3. **`get_anti_opponent_adjustments()`** — Adaptive exploitation system (adapted from bot5's `get_anti_bot4_adjustments`). Returns bluff frequency bonus, raise size bonus, call threshold delta, and trap defense delta based on opponent profile score and current board texture/spot.

4. **Anti-profile integration in `get_action()`** — Computes anti-profile adjustments after board texture analysis, applies them to:
   - Strong/medium decision thresholds (call threshold delta, trap defense delta)
   - Bluff frequency thresholds (river bluff, probe, semi-bluff all reduced by `bluff_freq_bonus`)
   - Blocker bluff frequency via `allow_low_frequency_blocker_bluff(req, ..., bluff_freq_bonus)`
   - Raise sizing via `choose_raise(anti_profile_bonus=...)`
   - River overbet enablement via `choose_raise(allow_river_overbet=...)`

5. **`allow_low_frequency_blocker_bluff()` with `bluff_freq_bonus`** — Extended from bot5's version. Adds opponent-exploitation-driven frequency bonus to blocker bluff threshold, making bluffs more frequent against exploitable opponents.

6. **`choose_raise()` with `anti_profile_bonus` and `allow_river_overbet`** — Extended with two new parameters from bot5. `anti_profile_bonus` adds to the raise ratio when exploiting opponent weaknesses. `allow_river_overbet` lifts the max ratio from 1.45 to 2.2 for river nut overbets.

### Structural Removals (Documented Regressions Fixed)

7. **Removed `bb_vs_raise` / `sb_vs_reraise` fixed-threshold logic** — These used hardcoded preflop_strength thresholds (0.72 for 3bet, 0.42 for call, 0.85 for 4bet) instead of simulation-based win_rate. This exact pattern caused regressions in v8, v9, and v11 (documented 3+ times in experience pool). Now falls through to the general simulation-based decision path, matching bot5 (Rank 1).

8. **Simplified exploitation framework** — Removed noisy `gift_balance`/`safe_exploitation_lambda` (documented in v12→v13 as adding complexity with unclear benefit). Replaced with direct anti-profile adjustments.

### Structurally Required Parameter Fixes (7+ Generations Documented)

9. **Sim counts**: 500/800/900 → 900/1200/1500 (matching bot5)
10. **VPIP/PFR priors**: 0.52/0.24 → 0.58/0.28 (matching bot5, documented since v12→v13)
11. **thin_cap**: 0.46+0.08w → 0.30/0.38 (matching bot5, documented since v8→v9)
12. **EQR values**: Air 0.68/0.56→0.72/0.62, Marginal pair 0.84/0.73→0.86/0.78 (matching bot5)
