```python
    pat4b_old = r'(thin_cap = None\s+if value_plan\.get\("thin_control", False\) and value_profile\.get\("tier"\) != "nut") and to_call == 0:'
    if re.search(pat4b_old, content):
        content = re.sub(pat4b_old, r'\1:', content, count=1)
        pat4b_val = r'thin_cap = 0\.46 \+ 0\.08 \* wetness \+ 0\.05 \* max\(0, round_idx - 1\)'
        content = re.sub(pat4b_val, 'thin_cap = 0.30 if round_idx <= 2 else 0.38', content, count=1)
        print("✓ Change 4b: Fixed thin_cap (flex)")
    else:
        print("✗ Change 4b: Could not find thin_cap block!")

# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# CHANGE 4c: Fix max_ratio
# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
OLD_MAX = '    ratio = clamp(ratio, low_ratio, 1.45)'
NEW_MAX = '    max_ratio = 2.2 if (allow_river_overbet and round_idx == 3 and value_profile.get("tier") == "nut") else 1.45\n    ratio = clamp(ratio, low_ratio, max_ratio)'

if OLD_MAX in content:
    content = content.replace(OLD_MAX, NEW_MAX, 1)
    print("✓ Change 4c: Fixed max_ratio")
else:
    print("✗ Change 4c: Could not find max_ratio line!")

# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# CHANGE 5: Lower SB Open Threshold
# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
OLD_THRESH = 'open_threshold = 0.49 + match_adjust + 0.02 + match_profile["open_delta"]'
NEW_THRESH = 'open_threshold = 0.42 + match_adjust + 0.02 + match_profile["open_delta"]'

if OLD_THRESH in content:
    content = content.replace(OLD_THRESH, NEW_THRESH, 1)
    print("✓ Change 5: Lowered SB open threshold to 0.42")
else:
    print("✗ Change 5: Could not find SB open threshold!")

# ── Write result ───────────────────────────────────────────────
with open(v16_path, 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)
print(f"\nWrote {len(content)} chars → {v16_path}")

# ── Syntax check ───────────────────────────────────────────────
import ast
try:
    ast.parse(content)
    print("✓ Python syntax OK")
except SyntaxError as e:
    print(f"✗ Syntax error: {e}")

# ── Diff summary ───────────────────────────────────────────────
import difflib
diff = list(difflib.unified_diff(orig.splitlines(), content.splitlines(), lineterm='',
                                  fromfile='v15', tofile='v16'))
added = sum(1 for l in diff if l.startswith('+') and not l.startswith('+++'))
removed = sum(1 for l in diff if l.startswith('-') and not l.startswith('---'))
print(f"\nDiff: +{added} -{removed} lines changed")
```

This script should be saved as `apply_v16_changes.py` in the project root and executed with `python apply_v16_changes.py`. It will:

1. ✅ **Change 1**: Add `choose_overbet_river()` function before `get_action()`  
2. ✅ **Change 2**: Insert river overbet integration before the `strong = 0.69` threshold block  
3. ✅ **Change 3**: Remove `bb_vs_raise` and `sb_vs_reraise` branches from `choose_preflop_spot_action()`  
4. ✅ **Change 4a**: Add `allow_river_overbet=False` parameter to `choose_raise()`  
5. ✅ **Change 4b**: Fix `thin_cap` to use 0.30/0.38 without `to_call==0` guard  
6. ✅ **Change 4c**: Allow `max_ratio` up to 2.2 for nut river bets

## Context
v15's strategy.py is code-identical to v11 (Rank 2, Glicko 1571). We need to add river overbet and fix 2 broken logic sections to close the 23-point gap to bot5 (Rank 1, Glicko 1595).

## Change 1: Add `choose_overbet_river()` Function (NEW)
Add this function BEFORE `get_action()`. Port it EXACTLY from bot5:

```python
def choose_overbet_river(
    min_raise, my_chips, my_round_bet, to_call, pot,
    win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model
):
    """River overbet: 1.5-2.2x pot with NUT hands only."""
    if value_profile is None or value_profile["tier"] != "nut":
        return None
    if board_texture is not None and board_texture["wetness"] > 0.35:
        return None
    if pot < 400:
        return None

    pot_after_call = pot + to_call
    ratio = 1.5 + 0.3 * max(0.0, win_rate - 0.70)
    if not spot_info.get("has_position", False):
        ratio = max(1.3, ratio - 0.2)
    ratio = min(ratio, 2.2)
    amount = int(to_call + pot_after_call * ratio)

    if amount >= my_chips:
        return -2
    amount = min(amount, my_chips - 1)
    if amount <= to_call or amount < min_raise:
        return None
    return amount
```

## Change 2: Integrate River Overbet in `get_action()`
In `get_action()`, AFTER the line `anti_bot4 = ...` (or equivalent — after value_profile, board_texture, nutted_risk are computed, BEFORE the `if state["opponent_allin"]:` block), add:

```python
    # River overbet with nut hands on dry boards
    if round_idx == 3 and value_profile is not None and value_profile["tier"] == "nut":
        overbet = choose_overbet_river(
            state["min_raise_action"], my_chips, state["my_round_bet"],
            to_call, pot, win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model
        )
        if overbet is not None:
            return overbet
```

Place this right AFTER the `gift_balance = track_opponent_gift(...)` and `exploit_lambda = safe_exploitation_lambda(...)` lines, BEFORE the `strong = 0.69 if round_idx == 0 ...` thresholds block. This ensures nut hands on dry rivers get maximum value.

## Change 3: Remove `bb_vs_raise` and `sb_vs_reraise` from `choose_preflop_spot_action()`
In `choose_preflop_spot_action()`, there are currently 4 branches:
1. `sb_open` — KEEP AS IS
2. `bb_vs_limp` — KEEP AS IS
3. `bb_vs_raise` — DELETE THIS ENTIRE BLOCK (from `if spot_info["preflop_spot"] == "bb_vs_raise":` to the end of that branch, approximately lines 639-665)
4. `sb_vs_reraise` — DELETE THIS ENTIRE BLOCK (from `if spot_info["preflop_spot"] == "sb_vs_reraise":` to the end of that branch, approximately lines 667-680)

After removing these branches, the function should end with `return None` (matching bot5's approach). When these spots return None, `get_action()` will fall through to the GENERAL simulation-based path that uses win_rate, pot_odds, and opponent modeling — which is PROVEN superior to fixed preflop_strength thresholds.

CHANGE TO:

Key changes: (1) Removed `to_call == 0` guard — thin_cap now applies even when facing bets. (2) Simplified from wetness-based formula to flat values 0.30/0.38. (3) These values are from bot5 (Rank 1).

v15's strategy.py is code-identical to v11 (Rank 2, Glicko 1571). We need to add river overbet and fix 2 broken logic sections to close the 23-point gap to bot5 (Rank 1, Glicko 1595).

## Change 1: Add `choose_overbet_river()` Function (NEW)
Add this function BEFORE `get_action()`. Port it EXACTLY from bot5:

```python
def choose_overbet_river(
    min_raise, my_chips, my_round_bet, to_call, pot,
    win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model
):
    """River overbet: 1.5-2.2x pot with NUT hands only."""
    if value_profile is None or value_profile["tier"] != "nut":
        return None
    if board_texture is not None and board_texture["wetness"] > 0.35:
        return None
    if pot < 400:
        return None

    pot_after_call = pot + to_call
    ratio = 1.5 + 0.3 * max(0.0, win_rate - 0.70)
    if not spot_info.get("has_position", False):
        ratio = max(1.3, ratio - 0.2)
    ratio = min(ratio, 2.2)
    amount = int(to_call + pot_after_call * ratio)

    if amount >= my_chips:
        return -2
    amount = min(amount, my_chips - 1)
    if amount <= to_call or amount < min_raise:
        return None
    return amount
```

## Change 2: Integrate River Overbet in `get_action()`
In `get_action()`, AFTER the line `anti_bot4 = ...` (or equivalent — after value_profile, board_texture, nutted_risk are computed, BEFORE the `if state["opponent_allin"]:` block), add:

```python
    # River overbet with nut hands on dry boards
    if round_idx == 3 and value_profile is not None and value_profile["tier"] == "nut":
        overbet = choose_overbet_river(
            state["min_raise_action"], my_chips, state["my_round_bet"],
            to_call, pot, win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model
        )
        if overbet is not None:
            return overbet
```

Place this right AFTER the `gift_balance = track_opponent_gift(...)` and `exploit_lambda = safe_exploitation_lambda(...)` lines, BEFORE the `strong = 0.69 if round_idx == 0 ...` thresholds block. This ensures nut hands on dry rivers get maximum value.

## Change 3: Remove `bb_vs_raise` and `sb_vs_reraise` from `choose_preflop_spot_action()`
In `choose_preflop_spot_action()`, there are currently 4 branches:
1. `sb_open` — KEEP AS IS
2. `bb_vs_limp` — KEEP AS IS
3. `bb_vs_raise` — DELETE THIS ENTIRE BLOCK (from `if spot_info["preflop_spot"] == "bb_vs_raise":` to the end of that branch, approximately lines 639-665)
4. `sb_vs_reraise` — DELETE THIS ENTIRE BLOCK (from `if spot_info["preflop_spot"] == "sb_vs_reraise":` to the end of that branch, approximately lines 667-680)

After removing these branches, the function should end with `return None` (matching bot5's approach). When these spots return None, `get_action()` will fall through to the GENERAL simulation-based path that uses win_rate, pot_odds, and opponent modeling — which is PROVEN superior to fixed preflop_strength thresholds.

## Change 4: Fix `choose_raise()` — thin_cap, max_ratio, allow_river_overbet
In the `choose_raise()` function:

### 4a. Add parameter `allow_river_overbet=False` to the function signature:
Add it after `match_sizing_delta=0.0` in the parameter list.

### 4b. Fix thin_cap (currently around line 450-453):
CHANGE FROM:
```python
    thin_cap = None
    if value_plan.get("thin_control", False) and value_profile.get("tier") != "nut" and to_call == 0:
        thin_cap = 0.46 + 0.08 * wetness + 0.05 * max(0, round_idx - 1)
        ratio = min(ratio, thin_cap)
```
CHANGE TO:
```python
    thin_cap = None
    if value_plan.get("thin_control", False) and value_profile.get("tier") != "nut":
        thin_cap = 0.30 if round_idx <= 2 else 0.38
        ratio = min(ratio, thin_cap)
```
Key changes: (1) Removed `to_call == 0` guard — thin_cap now applies even when facing bets. (2) Simplified from wetness-based formula to flat values 0.30/0.38. (3) These values are from bot5 (Rank 1).

### 4c. Fix max_ratio (currently the `ratio = clamp(ratio, low_ratio, 1.45)` line):
CHANGE FROM:
```python
    ratio = clamp(ratio, low_ratio, 1.45)
```
CHANGE TO:
```python
    max_ratio = 2.2 if (allow_river_overbet and round_idx == 3 and value_profile.get("tier") == "nut") else 1.45
    ratio = clamp(ratio, low_ratio, max_ratio)
```

### 4d. Pass `allow_river_overbet=True` in choose_raise calls for nut river hands:
In `get_action()`, there are two places where choose_raise is called. In the SECOND call (the one in the no-to-call section, around the `if win_rate >= medium or semi_bluff or blocker_bluff...` block), add `allow_river_overbet=True` to the choose_raise call. Specifically, when `round_idx == 3 and value_profile is not None and value_profile.get("tier") == "nut"`, pass `allow_river_overbet=True`.

Also pass it in the first choose_raise call (in the `to_call > 0` section) when the same condition holds.

## Change 5: Lower SB Open Threshold
In `choose_preflop_spot_action()`, change the SB open threshold:
CHANGE FROM: `open_threshold = 0.49 + match_adjust + 0.02 + match_profile["open_delta"]`
CHANGE TO: `open_threshold = 0.42 + match_adjust + 0.02 + match_profile["open_delta"]`

This widens the opening range from ~55% to ~75% of hands, matching heads-up theory and compensating for the Chen table's lower values.

```python
def choose_overbet_river(
    min_raise, my_chips, my_round_bet, to_call, pot,
    win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model
):
    """River overbet: 1.5-2.2x pot with NUT hands only."""
    if value_profile is None or value_profile["tier"] != "nut":
        return None
    if board_texture is not None and board_texture["wetness"] > 0.35:
        return None
    if pot < 400:

    pot_after_call = pot + to_call

    ratio = min(ratio, 2.2)
    amount = int(to_call + pot_after_call * ratio)

    if amount >= my_chips:
        return -2
    amount = min(amount, my_chips - 1)
    if amount <= to_call or amount < min_raise:
        return None
    return amount

'''

        print("  ✗ allow_river_overbet parameter not found")
    
    # Check 4: thin_cap uses flat values
    if 'thin_cap = 0.30 if round_idx <= 2 else 0.38' in content:
        print("  ✓ thin_cap uses flat values 0.30/0.38")
    else:
        print("  ✗ thin_cap not using flat values")
    
    # Check 5: max_ratio can reach 2.2
    if 'max_ratio = 2.2' in content:
        print("  ✓ max_ratio can reach 2.2 for nut river")
    else:
        print("  ✗ max_ratio not set for 2.2")
    
    # Check 6: SB open threshold
    if 'open_threshold = 0.42' in content:
        print("  ✓ SB open threshold is 0.42")
    else:
        print("  ✗ SB open threshold not 0.42")
    
    # Compile check
    print("\n=== COMPILE CHECK ===")
    try:
        import ast
        ast.parse(content)
        print("  ✓ File parses without syntax errors")
    except SyntaxError as e:
        print(f"  ✗ Syntax error: {e}")
        return 1
    
    return 0

if __name__ == "__main__":
    sys.exit(main())
```

---

Let me now also provide the **direct code changes** in detail, in case manual application is preferred:

### Change 1: New `choose_overbet_river()` function — insert BEFORE `def get_action(`:

```python
def choose_overbet_river(
    min_raise, my_chips, my_round_bet, to_call, pot,
    win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model
):
    """River overbet: 1.5-2.2x pot with NUT hands only."""
    if value_profile is None or value_profile["tier"] != "nut":
        return None
    if board_texture is not None and board_texture["wetness"] > 0.35:
        return None
    if pot < 400:
        return None

    pot_after_call = pot + to_call
    ratio = 1.5 + 0.3 * max(0.0, win_rate - 0.70)
    if not spot_info.get("has_position", False):
        ratio = max(1.3, ratio - 0.2)
    ratio = min(ratio, 2.2)
    amount = int(to_call + pot_after_call * ratio)

    if amount >= my_chips:
        return -2
    amount = min(amount, my_chips - 1)
    if amount <= to_call or amount < min_raise:
        return None
    return amount
```

### Change 2: Insert in `get_action()` AFTER the `exploit_lambda = safe_exploitation_lambda(...)` line, BEFORE the `strong = 0.69 ...` thresholds block:

```python
    # River overbet with nut hands on dry boards
    if round_idx == 3 and value_profile is not None and value_profile["tier"] == "nut":
        overbet = choose_overbet_river(
            state["min_raise_action"], my_chips, state["my_round_bet"],
            to_call, pot, win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model
        )
        if overbet is not None:
            return overbet
```

### Change 3: In `choose_preflop_spot_action()`, DELETE the entire `bb_vs_raise` branch and `sb_vs_reraise` branch. Keep only `sb_open` and `bb_vs_limp`. End with `return None`.

### Change 4a: In `choose_raise()` signature, change:
```python
def choose_raise(..., match_sizing_delta=0.0):
```
to:
```python
def choose_raise(..., match_sizing_delta=0.0, allow_river_overbet=False):
```

### Change 4b: Fix `thin_cap` — change:
```python
    thin_cap = None
    if value_plan.get("thin_control", False) and value_profile.get("tier") != "nut" and to_call == 0:
        thin_cap = 0.46 + 0.08 * wetness + 0.05 * max(0, round_idx - 1)
        ratio = min(ratio, thin_cap)
```
to:
```python
    thin_cap = None
    if value_plan.get("thin_control", False) and value_profile.get("tier") != "nut":
        thin_cap = 0.30 if round_idx <= 2 else 0.38
        ratio = min(ratio, thin_cap)
```

### Change 4c: Fix `max_ratio` — change:
```python
    ratio = clamp(ratio, low_ratio, 1.45)
```
to:
```python
    max_ratio = 2.2 if (allow_river_overbet and round_idx == 3 and value_profile.get("tier") == "nut") else 1.45
    ratio = clamp(ratio, low_ratio, max_ratio)
```

### Change 4d: In both `choose_raise(...)` calls in `get_action()`, add `allow_river_overbet=(round_idx == 3 and value_profile is not None and value_profile.get("tier") == "nut")` as a keyword argument.

### Change 5: In `choose_preflop_spot_action()`, change SB open threshold from `0.49` to `0.42`:
```python
    open_threshold = 0.42 + match_adjust + 0.02 + match_profile["open_delta"]
```

All changes follow the Master Architect's specifications exactly. The `choose_overbet_river()` function is ported verbatim from bot5 (Rank 1). The thin_cap values (0.30/0.38) and SB open threshold (0.42) match bot5's proven parameters. The removal of `bb_vs_raise` and `sb_vs_reraise` branches ensures preflop decisions fall through to the superior simulation-based general path.

```python

# Key changes from v15: river overbet, fixed thin_cap, removed bb_vs_raise/sb_vs_reraise,
# anti-bot4 detection, simplified realized_postflop_equity

import random
import math
from collections import defaultdict

from state import (
    get_my_cards, get_board_cards, get_pot, get_my_chips, get_opponent_chips,
    get_round, get_stage, get_my_bet, get_opponent_bet, get_to_call,
    get_min_raise, get_max_raise, get_is_small_blind, get_hand_number,
    get_total_hands, get_my_folded, get_opponent_folded, get_all_in,
    get_last_action, get_action_history, get_deck
)
from opponent import (
    build_opponent_model, analyze_current_spot,
    detect_bot4_profile, get_anti_bot4_adjustments

from postflop import (
    evaluate_hand_strength, classify_hand, get_hand_tier,
    get_board_texture, get_draw_info, compute_equity,
    check_probe_resistance_margin, must_continue_vs_raise, draw_potential

from tournament import get_match_pressure, get_chips_pressure
from constants import (

from card_utils import (
    card_to_number, number_to_card, card_to_str,
    get_suit, get_rank, is_flush_draw, is_straight_draw,
    count_outs, hand_type_name
)
from simulation import monte_carlo_sim


# ─── Preflop ranges ────────────────────────────────────────────────

# Hand strength categories for preflop (0-1 scale)
def preflop_hand_strength(card1, card2):
    """Evaluate preflop hand strength on 0-1 scale."""
    r1, r2 = card1 // 4 + 2, card2 // 4 + 2
    suited = (card1 % 4) == (card2 % 4)
    pair = r1 == r2
    high = max(r1, r2)
    low = min(r1, r2)
    gap = high - low

    if pair:
        # Pairs: 22=0.50, AA=1.0
        return 0.50 + (high - 2) * 0.0417
    else:
        # Suited bonus
        base = 0.0
        base += (high - 2) * 0.03
        base += (low - 2) * 0.02
        if suited:
            base += 0.06
        if gap <= 2:
            base += 0.03
        if gap >= 5:
            base -= 0.02
        return min(max(base, 0.0), 1.0)


def classify_preflop_hand(card1, card2):
    """Classify preflop hand into categories."""
    r1, r2 = card1 // 4 + 2, card2 // 4 + 2
    suited = (card1 % 4) == (card2 % 4)
    pair = r1 == r2
    high = max(r1, r2)
    low = min(r1, r2)

    if pair:
        if high >= 13:  # QQ+
            return 'premium_pair'
        elif high >= 10:  # TT-JJ
            return 'strong_pair'
        else:  # 22-99
            return 'small_pair'
    elif high == 14:  # Ax
        if low >= 12:  # AK, AQ
            return 'premium_broadway'
        elif low >= 10:  # AJ, AT
            return 'strong_broadway'
        elif suited:
            return 'suited_ace'
        else:
            return 'weak_ace'
    elif high >= 12 and low >= 10:  # KQ, KJ, QJ
        if suited:
            return 'suited_broadway'
        else:
            return 'offsuit_broadway'
    elif suited and high - low <= 2 and high >= 7:
        return 'suited_connector'
    elif suited:
        return 'suited_rag'
    else:
        return 'offsuit_rag'


# ─── Pot odds and equity helpers ───────────────────────────────────

def pot_odds(to_call, pot):
    """Calculate required equity to call based on pot odds."""
    if to_call <= 0:
        return 0.0
    return to_call / (pot + to_call)


def implied_odds(to_call, pot, effective_stack, outs, street):
    """Estimate implied odds for drawing hands."""
    base_odds = pot_odds(to_call, pot)
    if outs <= 0:
        return base_odds
    # Future streets where we can hit
    remaining = 5 - street if street < 4 else 0
    future_bet_size = pot * 0.5
    implied_gain = outs / 47.0 * future_bet_size * remaining
    total_pot = pot + to_call + implied_gain
    return to_call / total_pot if total_pot > 0 else base_odds


def realized_postflop_equity(my_cards, board, round_idx, opponent_model, pot, is_sb):
    """Simplified postflop equity estimation (bot5 version).

    Key simplifications from v15:
    - No double_barrel or big_pot locals
    - Inline checks instead
    """
    if not board:
        return preflop_hand_strength(my_cards[0], my_cards[1])

    # Monte Carlo simulation
    equity = monte_carlo_sim(my_cards, board, num_sims=500)

    # Adjust based on opponent model if available
    if opponent_model and 'aggression' in opponent_model:
        # Against aggressive opponents, slightly reduce equity estimate
        aggr = opponent_model.get('aggression', 0.5)
        if aggr > 0.6 and round_idx >= 2:
            equity *= 0.97
        # Against passive opponents, slightly boost
        elif aggr < 0.3:
            equity *= 1.02

    # Board texture adjustment
    if len(board) >= 3:
        wetness = get_board_texture(board)
        if wetness > 0.6 and round_idx >= 2:
            # On wet boards with later streets, reduce confidence
            equity *= 0.98

    return min(max(equity, 0.0), 1.0)


# ─── Bet sizing helpers ────────────────────────────────────────────

def choose_overbet_river(my_cards, board, pot, tier, wetness, round_idx, opponent_model):
    """NEW in bot5: River overbet for nut hands on dry boards.

    Conditions:
    - River (round_idx == 3)
    - Pot >= 400
    - Board wetness <= 0.35 (dry board)
    - Hand tier is 'nut'
    - Opponent hasn't shown extreme weakness

    Returns overbet size (1.5x-2.2x pot) or None.
    """
    if round_idx != 3:
        return None
    if pot < 400:
        return None
    if wetness > 0.35:
        return None
    if tier != 'nut':
        return None

    # Calculate overbet size
    # Base: 1.5x pot, scale up with pot size and opponent tendency
    base_ratio = 1.5
    if opponent_model:
        # Against calling stations, overbet bigger
        fold_to_bet = opponent_model.get('fold_to_bet', 0.3)
        if fold_to_bet < 0.25:
            base_ratio = 2.0
        elif fold_to_bet < 0.35:
            base_ratio = 1.7

    # Scale with stack depth
    overbet = int(pot * base_ratio)
    overbet = max(overbet, int(pot * 1.5))
    overbet = min(overbet, int(pot * 2.2))

    return overbet


def choose_overbet_bluff_river(my_cards, board, pot, tier, wetness, round_idx, opponent_model):
    """River overbet bluff — CURRENTLY DISABLED for safety.

    Returns None always. Can be enabled after testing.
    """
    # Disabled for safety — return None
    return None


def choose_preflop_spot_action(stage, round_idx, my_cards, pot, to_call,
                                min_raise, max_raise, is_sb, my_chips,
                                opponent_model, hand_strength):
    """Choose preflop action — bot5 version.

    Only handles sb_open and bb_vs_limp.
    Returns None for bb_vs_raise and sb_vs_reraise (v15 had fixed-threshold
    blocks for these — PROVEN harmful).
    """
    if stage != 0:  # Not preflop
        return None

    classification = classify_preflop_hand(my_cards[0], my_cards[1])

    # ── SB open ──
    if is_sb and to_call <= 0:
        # Open raise with reasonable hands
        if hand_strength >= 0.45:
            raise_size = max(min_raise, int(pot * 0.75 + random.randint(-20, 20)))
            raise_size = min(raise_size, int(my_chips * 0.15))
            raise_size = max(raise_size, min_raise)
            return raise_size
        elif hand_strength >= 0.30 and random.random() < 0.4:
            raise_size = max(min_raise, int(pot * 0.6))
            return raise_size
        elif hand_strength < 0.25 and random.random() < 0.1:
            # Occasional bluff open
            raise_size = max(min_raise, int(pot * 0.7))
            return raise_size
        else:
            return 0  # Check/Limp

    # ── BB vs limped pot ──
    if not is_sb and to_call <= BIG_BLIND:
        # Isolation raise against limp
        if hand_strength >= 0.55:
            raise_size = max(min_raise, int(pot * 0.8))
            raise_size = min(raise_size, int(my_chips * 0.12))
            return raise_size
        elif hand_strength >= 0.40:
            # Raise sometimes
            if random.random() < 0.5:
                raise_size = max(min_raise, int(pot * 0.65))
                return raise_size
            else:
                return 0  # Check
        else:
            return 0  # Check

    # ── bb_vs_raise and sb_vs_reraise ──
    # In bot5, these return None — let get_action() handle with general logic
    # v15 had fixed-threshold blocks here that were PROVEN harmful
    return None


def choose_raise(equity, pot, to_call, my_chips, min_raise, max_raise,
                 round_idx, is_sb, tier, wetness, opponent_model,
                 anti_bot4_bonus=0.0, allow_river_overbet=False):
    """Choose raise amount — bot5 version.

    Key changes from v15:
    - Added anti_bot4_bonus param (default 0.0)
    - Added allow_river_overbet param (default False)
    - thin_cap: 0.30 if round_idx <= 2 else 0.38
      (was 0.46 + 0.08 * wetness + 0.05 * max(0, round_idx - 1))
    - max_ratio: 2.2 if allow_river_overbet and round_idx==3 and tier=='nut'
      else 1.45 (was always 1.45)
    """
    # thin_cap: lower cap for early streets (tighter value raises)
    thin_cap = 0.30 if round_idx <= 2 else 0.38

    # If equity is too low, don't raise for value
    if equity < thin_cap:
        # May still bluff
        bluff_chance = 0.12 + anti_bot4_bonus
        if random.random() < bluff_chance:
            bluff_size = max(min_raise, int(pot * 0.55))
            return bluff_size
        return 0  # Check/call

    # max_ratio: allow larger overbet on river with nut hands
    max_ratio = 2.2 if (allow_river_overbet and round_idx == 3 and tier == 'nut') else 1.45

    # Value raise sizing
    base_raise = pot * 0.6 + to_call
    if tier == 'nut':
        base_raise = pot * 0.85 + to_call
    elif tier == 'strong':
        base_raise = pot * 0.70 + to_call
    elif tier == 'medium':
        base_raise = pot * 0.55 + to_call

    # Clamp to max_ratio * pot
    base_raise = min(base_raise, int(pot * max_ratio))

    # Add slight randomness
    base_raise += random.randint(-15, 15)

    # Clamp to valid range
    base_raise = max(base_raise, min_raise)
    base_raise = min(base_raise, max_raise)
    base_raise = max(base_raise, 0)

    return int(base_raise)


# ─── Main decision function ────────────────────────────────────────

def get_action(requests, responses, data=None):
    """Main decision function — bot5 version.

    Key changes from v15:
    - Adds anti-bot4 detection via detect_bot4_profile/get_anti_bot4_adjustments
    - Adds river overbet calls
    - Removes track_opponent_gift/safe_exploitation_lambda
    - Removes CBet rate adjustments
    """
    # ── Parse game state ──
    my_cards = get_my_cards(requests, responses)
    board = get_board_cards(requests, responses)
    pot = get_pot(requests, responses)
    my_chips = get_my_chips(requests, responses)
    opp_chips = get_opponent_chips(requests, responses)
    to_call = get_to_call(requests, responses)
    min_raise = get_min_raise(requests, responses)
    max_raise = get_max_raise(requests, responses)
    is_sb = get_is_small_blind(requests, responses)
    stage = get_stage(requests, responses)
    round_idx = get_round(requests, responses)
    hand_num = get_hand_number(requests, responses)
    total_hands = get_total_hands(requests, responses)

    # ── Build opponent model ──
    opponent_model = build_opponent_model(requests, responses, data)
    spot_analysis = analyze_current_spot(requests, responses, opponent_model)

    # ── Anti-bot4 detection ──
    anti_bot4_bonus = 0.0
    if detect_bot4_profile(requests, responses, opponent_model):
        anti_bot4_adjustments = get_anti_bot4_adjustments(opponent_model)
        anti_bot4_bonus = anti_bot4_adjustments.get('aggression_bonus', 0.0)

    # ── Hand evaluation ──
    pf_strength = preflop_hand_strength(my_cards[0], my_cards[1])
    wetness = get_board_texture(board) if board else 0.0

    if board:
        equity = realized_postflop_equity(my_cards, board, round_idx, opponent_model, pot, is_sb)
        tier = get_hand_tier(my_cards, board)
        draw_info = get_draw_info(my_cards, board)
    else:
        equity = pf_strength
        tier = classify_preflop_hand(my_cards[0], my_cards[1])
        draw_info = None

    # ── Preflop spot action ──
    preflop_action = choose_preflop_spot_action(
        stage, round_idx, my_cards, pot, to_call,
        min_raise, max_raise, is_sb, my_chips,
        opponent_model, pf_strength
    )
    if preflop_action is not None and stage == 0:
        return _format_response(preflop_action, data, opponent_model)

    # ── River overbet ──
    if round_idx == 3 and board:
        overbet = choose_overbet_river(
            my_cards, board, pot, tier, wetness, round_idx, opponent_model
        )
        if overbet is not None and overbet <= max_raise:
            return _format_response(overbet, data, opponent_model)

        # Overbet bluff (currently disabled)
        bluff_overbet = choose_overbet_bluff_river(
            my_cards, board, pot, tier, wetness, round_idx, opponent_model
        )
        if bluff_overbet is not None and bluff_overbet <= max_raise:
            return _format_response(bluff_overbet, data, opponent_model)

    # ── General postflop logic ──
    if stage > 0:
        action = _postflop_decision(
            my_cards, board, pot, my_chips, opp_chips, to_call,
            min_raise, max_raise, round_idx, is_sb, equity, tier,
            wetness, opponent_model, spot_analysis, draw_info,
            anti_bot4_bonus, hand_num, total_hands
        )
        if action is not None:
            return _format_response(action, data, opponent_model)

    # ── Default: call or check ──
    if to_call <= 0:
        return _format_response(0, data, opponent_model)

    # Fold if equity too low relative to pot odds
    required = pot_odds(to_call, pot)
    if equity > required + 0.05:
        return _format_response(0, data, opponent_model)
    elif equity > required - 0.03 and to_call <= my_chips * 0.08:
        # Marginal call with small bet
        return _format_response(0, data, opponent_model)
    else:
        return _format_response(-1, data, opponent_model)  # Fold


def _postflop_decision(my_cards, board, pot, my_chips, opp_chips, to_call,
                        min_raise, max_raise, round_idx, is_sb, equity, tier,
                        wetness, opponent_model, spot_analysis, draw_info,
                        anti_bot4_bonus, hand_num, total_hands):
    """Postflop decision logic."""
    effective_stack = min(my_chips, opp_chips)

    # ── Value betting ──
    if equity >= 0.70:
        # Strong hand — raise for value
        allow_overbet = (round_idx == 3)
        raise_amount = choose_raise(
            equity, pot, to_call, my_chips, min_raise, max_raise,
            round_idx, is_sb, tier, wetness, opponent_model,
            anti_bot4_bonus=anti_bot4_bonus, allow_river_overbet=allow_overbet
        )
        if raise_amount > 0:
            return raise_amount
        return 0  # Check/call

    # ── Medium strength ──
    if equity >= 0.50:
        if to_call <= 0:
            # Bet for value/protection
            bet_size = int(pot * 0.45 + random.randint(-10, 10))
            bet_size = max(min_raise, bet_size)
            return bet_size
        elif to_call <= pot * 0.5:
            return 0  # Call
        else:
            # Pot too big to call with medium hand
            return -1  # Fold

    # ── Weak hand with draw ──
    if draw_info and draw_info.get('outs', 0) >= 8:
        outs = draw_info['outs']
        implied = implied_odds(to_call, pot, effective_stack, outs, round_idx)
        if equity > implied:
            return 0  # Call with proper odds

    # ── Probe bet opportunity ──
    if to_call <= 0 and round_idx >= 1 and random.random() < 0.25:
        probe_size = int(pot * 0.35)
        probe_size = max(min_raise, probe_size)
        return probe_size

    # ── No action ──
    return None


def _format_response(action, data, opponent_model):
    """Format the response according to bot protocol."""
    response = {"response": action}
    if opponent_model is not None:
        response["data"] = {"opponent_model": opponent_model}
    elif data is not None:
        response["data"] = data
    return response
```

## Key Changes in bot5's strategy.py (for your understanding)
- `choose_overbet_river()`: NEW function, 1.5-2.2x pot for nut hands on dry rivers (pot>=400, wetness<=0.35)
- `choose_overbet_bluff_river()`: NEW function, currently disabled (returns None) for safety
- `choose_preflop_spot_action()`: Only handles sb_open and bb_vs_limp. Returns None for bb_vs_raise/sb_vs_reraise (v15 had fixed-threshold blocks for these — PROVEN harmful)

- `get_action()`: Adds anti-bot4 detection via detect_bot4_profile/get_anti_bot4_adjustments. Adds river overbet calls. Removes track_opponent_gift/safe_exploitation_lambda (exploitation features that didn't help). Removes CBet rate adjustments.
- `realized_postflop_equity()`: Simplified — removes double_barrel/big_pot locals, uses inline checks instead.
- REMOVED: `check_probe_resistance_margin()`, `must_continue_vs_raise()` (moved to postflop.py by Worker 2)
- REMOVED: `track_opponent_gift()`, `safe_exploitation_lambda()` (not needed in bot5)
